    Use correct (cross-version) mode for READ_APPEND
    
    The documented mode string for append-with-read is "a+" for Python 2,
    Python 3, and glibc. "ra" may be an unofficial extension allowed in
    Python 2 by accident.

commit e312a84dc5db6ce070cb64476421931817fbb213
Author: Thomas Jollans <tjol@tjol.eu>
Date:   2018-10-13 21:14:06 +0200

    Python 3: Support for non-UTF8 filenames
    
    Non-UTF8 file names are more difficult to handle in Python 3 when
    combined with GTK+3/Gio. We must now distinguish between strings that
    are treated as file names -- these may contain surrage codepoints
    representing undecodable bytes -- and strings that are for display in
    the user interface.
    
    One reason this is necessary is that PyGObject refuses to pass surrogate
    codepoints to GTK+. However, it allows passing bytes (rather than str)
    to functions expecting file names.
    
    The helper functions sunflower.common.disp_fn() and
    sunflower.common.encode_fn() know how to move between these two worlds.

commit b3478f1a8dc34b6403beba7f8afbef7ced822f63
Author: Thomas Jollans <tjol@tjol.eu>
Date:   2018-10-13 17:43:34 +0200

    Ported to Python 3
    
     - This is not intended to support obsolete Python 2 (not that that
       would be so hard, it's only that it's 2018)
     - Moved everything to a package 'sunflower' and used relative
       imports for most things. This means there's no need to worry
       about clashing with built-in or third-party module names
     - THIS BREAKS ALL THIRD-PARTY PLUGINS
     - Most calls to map() and filter() are replaced with list
       comprehensions or loops. By and large the code assumed
       eager evaluation of these.
     - xrange etc. replaced with the Python 3 versions

commit 506abc0b60d171e2abd09c60861f0d4b327da2e7
Author: Mladen Mijatov <meaneye.rcf@gmail.com>
Date:   2018-05-05 16:24:20 +0300

    Main window: Fixed warning with geometry parsing.
    
    We will no longer attempt to position the window for number of reasons.
    Most important one is that GTK+ geometry handling has been deprecated
    since 3.20 version and in addition to that geometry handling is window
    management job.
    
    Instead we set default size and let the rest be handled by the system
    itself.

    Target 'dist-deb' was failing with untar error:
    
    ```
    tar: .//build/sunflower-0.3-60.tar: Cannot open: No such file or directory
    ```

commit d36df3417a47eac88fd1fe738ea9a3f630079de6
Author: Mladen Mijatov <meaneye.rcf@gmail.com>
Date:   2016-01-13 05:02:24 +0100

    Fixed issue with canceling disk usage calculation.
    
    Issue was avoided by dedicating threads per tab or parent object.
    Rationale behind such solution is the fact complexity of code far
    outweighs marginal performance benefits gained by calculating directory
    size once instead of per object. Real world usage of such cases where
    two threads are started for same path are going to be fairly limited and
    even then operating system cache makes sure operations on already probed
    inodes are faster.

1	1	application/gui/main_window.py
4	3	application/plugins/file_list/file_list.py
69	28	application/tools/disk_usage.py

commit 168f4eac9bb271f5e11622624c028f249d144931
Author: MeanEYE.rcf <meaneye.rcf@gmail.com>
Date:   2014-01-19 01:49:51 +0100

    Plugins: File list: If enabled compare strings with attention to numbers.
    
    If number sensitive sort is turned off files would sorted like this:
    
    1.txt
    10.txt
    2.txt
    
    With number sensitive sort, order is proper and expected:
    
    1.txt
    2.txt
    10.txt
    
    We achieve this by splitting string into list of characters and numbers and
    then compare list itself using built-in `cmp` function.
    
    As this process uses regular expressions it's turned off by default to avoid
    slowdowns in big directories.

13	4	application/plugins/file_list/plugin.py

commit 57550b8c6efeb8271bd3eb16605dcc3418e08160
Author: MeanEYE.rcf <meaneye.rcf@gmail.com>
Date:   2012-11-02 16:40:59 +0100

    Plugins: File list: Fixed racing condition when loading items for a specific directory.
    
    GTK is not thread safe. Problem occured when separate thread was
    created to handle remaining items. On occasion, due to different file
    system speeds, racing condition would occur causing program to crash.
    
    After properly locking main thread to update list store issue
    was mitigated and additionally we gained some loading speed as
    a result of threads working properly.

2	1	application/plugins/file_list/plugin.py
